   eipen tis ex auton, idios auton prophetes, Kretes aei pseustai, kaka
   theria, gasteres argai·

   he marturia haute estin alethes. di' hen aitian elenche autous
   apotomos, hina hugiainosin en te pistei,

   me prosechontes Ioudaikois muthois kai entolais anthropon
   apostrephomenon ten aletheian.

   ?panta kathara tois katharois· tois de memiammenois kai apistois ouden
   katharon, alla memiantai auton kai ho nous kai he suneidesis.

   theon homologousin eidenai, tois de ergois arnountai, bdeluktoi ontes
   kai apeitheis kai pros pan ergon agathon adokimoi.
     __________________________________________________________________

   Su de lalei ha prepei te hugiainouse didaskalia.

   presbutas nephalious einai, semnous, sophronas, hugiainontas te pistei,
   te agape, te hupomone.

   Presbutidas hosautos en katastemati hieroprepeis, me diabolous ?mede
   oino pollo dedoulomenas, kalodidaskalous,

   hina ?sophronizosi tas neas philandrous einai, philoteknous,

   sophronas, hagnas, ?oikourgous, agathas, hupotassomenas tois idiois
   andrasin, hina me ho logos tou theou blasphemetai.

   Tous neoterous hosautos parakalei sophronein·

   peri panta seauton parechomenos tupon kalon ergon, en te didaskalia
   ?aphthorian, ?semnoteta,

   logon hugie akatagnoston, hina ho ex enantias entrape meden echon
   ?legein peri hemon? phaulon.

   Doulous idiois despotais hupotassesthai en pasin, euarestous einai, me
   antilegontas,

   me nosphizomenous, alla ?pasan pistin? endeiknumenous agathen, hina ten
   didaskalian ?ten tou soteros hemon theou kosmosin en pasin.

   Epephane gar he charis tou ?theou soterios pasin anthropois

   paideuousa hemas, hina arnesamenoi ten asebeian kai tas kosmikas
   epithumias sophronos kai dikaios kai eusebos zesomen en to nun aioni,

   prosdechomenoi ten makarian elpida kai epiphaneian tes doxes tou
   megalou theou kai soteros hemon ?Iesou Christou?,

   hos edoken heauton huper hemon hina lutrosetai hemas apo pases anomias
   kai katharise heauto laon periousion, zeloten kalon ergon.

   Tauta lalei kai parakalei kai elenche meta pases epitages· medeis sou
   periphroneito.
     __________________________________________________________________

   Hupomimneske autous ?archais exousiais hupotassesthai peitharchein,
   pros pan ergon agathon hetoimous einai,

   medena blasphemein, amachous einai, epieikeis, pasan endeiknumenous
   prauteta pros pantas anthropous.

   emen gar pote kai hemeis anoetoi, apeitheis, planomenoi, douleuontes
   epithumiais kai hedonais poikilais, en kakia kai phthono diagontes,
   stugetoi, misountes allelous.

   hote de he chrestotes kai he philanthropia epephane tou soteros hemon
   theou,

   ouk ex ergon ton en dikaiosune ?ha epoiesamen hemeis alla kata ?to
   autou eleos? esosen hemas dia loutrou palingenesias kai anakainoseos
   pneumatos hagiou,

   hou execheen eph' hemas plousios dia Iesou Christou tou soteros hemon,

   hina dikaiothentes te ekeinou chariti kleronomoi ?genethomen kat'
   elpida zoes aioniou.

   Pistos ho logos, kai peri touton boulomai se diabebaiousthai, hina
   phrontizosin kalon ergon proistasthai hoi pepisteukotes theo. tauta
   ?estin kala kai ophelima tois anthropois·

   moras de zeteseis kai genealogias kai ?ereis kai machas nomikas
   periistaso, eisin gar anopheleis kai mataioi.

   hairetikon anthropon meta mian kai deuteran nouthesian paraitou,

   eidos hoti exestraptai ho toioutos kai hamartanei, on autokatakritos.

   Hotan pempso Arteman pros se e Tuchikon, spoudason elthein pros me eis
   Nikopolin, ekei gar kekrika paracheimasai.

   zenan ton nomikon kai ?Apollon spoudaios propempson, hina meden autois
   leipe.

   manthanetosan de kai hoi hemeteroi kalon ergon proistasthai eis tas
   anankaias chreias, hina me osin akarpoi.

   Aspazontai se hoi met' emou pantes. aspasai tous philountas hemas en
   pistei. he charis meta panton ?humon.
     __________________________________________________________________

                                 PROS PhILEMONA
     __________________________________________________________________

   Paulos desmios Christou Iesou kai Timotheos ho adelphos Philemoni to
   agapeto kai sunergo hemon

   kai Apphia te ?adelphe kai Archippo to sustratiote hemon kai te kat'
   oikon sou ekklesia·

   charis humin kai eirene apo theou patros hemon kai kuriou Iesou
   Christou.

   Eucharisto to theo mou pantote mneian sou poioumenos epi ton proseuchon
   mou,

   akouon sou ten agapen kai ten pistin hen echeis ?pros ton kurion Iesoun
   kai eis pantas tous hagious,

   hopos he koinonia tes pisteos sou energes genetai en epignosei pantos
   agathou ?tou en hemin eis ?Christon·

   ?charan gar ?pollen eschon? kai paraklesin epi te agape sou, hoti ta
   splanchna ton hagion anapepautai dia sou, adelphe.

   Dio, pollen en Christo parresian echon epitassein soi to anekon,

   dia ten agapen mallon parakalo, toioutos on hos Paulos presbutes nuni
   de kai desmios ?Christou Iesou?--

   parakalo se peri tou emou teknou, hon egennesa en tois ?desmois
   Onesimon,

   ton pote soi achreston nuni ?de soi kai emoi euchreston,

   hon anepempsa ?soi auton, tout' estin ta ema splanchna?·

   hon ego eboulomen pros emauton katechein, hina huper sou ?moi diakone?
   en tois desmois tou euangeliou,

   choris de tes ses gnomes ouden ethelesa poiesai, hina me hos kata
   ananken to agathon sou e alla kata hekousion·

   tacha gar dia touto echoristhe pros horan hina aionion auton apeches,

   ouketi hos doulon alla huper doulon, adelphon agapeton, malista emoi,
   poso de mallon soi kai en sarki kai en kurio.

   Ei oun me echeis koinonon, proslabou auton hos eme.

   ei de ti edikesen se e opheilei, touto emoi ?elloga·

   ego Paulos egrapsa te eme cheiri, ego apotiso· hina me lego soi hoti
   kai seauton moi prosopheileis.

   nai, adelphe, ego sou onaimen en kurio· anapauson mou ta splanchna en
   ?Christo.

   pepoithos te hupakoe sou egrapsa soi, eidos hoti kai huper ?ha lego
   poieseis.

   hama de kai hetoimaze moi xenian, elpizo gar hoti dia ton proseuchon
   humon charisthesomai humin.

   ?Aspazetai se Epaphras ho sunaichmalotos mou en Christo Iesou,

   Markos, Aristarchos, Demas, Loukas, hoi sunergoi mou.

   He charis tou ?kuriou Iesou Christou meta tou pneumatos ?humon.
     __________________________________________________________________

                                 PROS EBRAIOUS
     __________________________________________________________________

   Polumeros kai polutropos palai ho theos lalesas tois patrasin en tois
   prophetais

   ep' eschatou ton hemeron touton elalesen hemin en huio, hon etheken
   kleronomon panton, di' hou kai ?epoiesen tous aionas?·

   hos on apaugasma tes doxes kai charakter tes hupostaseos autou, pheron
   te ta panta to rhemati tes dunameos, ?di' hautou? katharismon ?ton
   hamartion poiesamenos? ekathisen en dexia tes megalosunes en hupselois,

   tosouto kreitton genomenos ton angelon hoso diaphoroteron par' autous
   kekleronomeken onoma.

   Tini gar eipen pote ton angelon· Huios mou ei su, ego semeron gegenneka
   se, kai palin· Ego esomai auto eis patera, kai autos estai moi eis
   huion;

   hotan de palin eisagage ton prototokon eis ten oikoumenen, legei· Kai
   proskunesatosan auto pantes angeloi theou.

   kai pros men tous angelous legei· Ho poion tous angelous autou
   pneumata, kai tous leitourgous autou puros phloga·

   pros de ton huion· Ho thronos sou ho theos eis ton aiona tou aionos,
   ?kai he rhabdos tes euthutetos? rhabdos tes basileias ?sou.

   egapesas dikaiosunen kai emisesas anomian· dia touto echrisen se ho
   theos, ho theos sou, elaion agalliaseos para tous metochous sou·

   kai· Su kat' archas, kurie, ten gen ethemeliosas, kai erga ton cheiron
   sou eisin hoi ouranoi·

   autoi apolountai, su de diameneis· kai pantes hos himation
   palaiothesontai,

   kai hosei peribolaion helixeis autous, ?hos himation? kai allagesontai·
   su de ho autos ei, kai ta ete sou ouk ekleipsousin.

   pros tina de ton angelon eireken pote· Kathou ek dexion mou heos an tho
   tous echthrous sou hupopodion ton podon sou;

   ouchi pantes eisin leitourgika pneumata eis diakonian apostellomena dia
   tous mellontas kleronomein soterian;
     __________________________________________________________________

   Dia touto dei perissoteros ?prosechein hemas? tois akoustheisin, mepote
   pararuomen.

   ei gar ho di' angelon laletheis logos egeneto bebaios, kai pasa
   parabasis kai parakoe elaben endikon misthapodosian,

   pos hemeis ekpheuxometha telikautes amelesantes soterias, hetis, archen
   labousa laleisthai dia tou kuriou, hupo ton akousanton eis hemas
   ebebaiothe,

   sunepimarturountos tou theou semeiois te kai terasin kai poikilais
   dunamesin kai pneumatos hagiou merismois kata ten autou thelesin;

   Ou gar angelois hupetaxen ten oikoumenen ten mellousan, peri hes
   laloumen·

   diemarturato de pou tis legon· Ti estin anthropos hoti mimneske autou,
   e huios anthropou hoti episkepte auton;

   elattosas auton brachu ti par' angelous, doxe kai time estephanosas
   ?auton,

   panta hupetaxas hupokato ton podon autou· en ?to gar? ?hupotaxai ta
   panta ouden apheken auto anupotakton. nun de oupo horomen auto ta panta
   hupotetagmena·

   ton de brachu ti par' angelous elattomenon blepomen Iesoun dia to
   pathema tou thanatou doxe kai time estephanomenon, hopos ?choris theou
   huper pantos geusetai thanatou.

   Eprepen gar auto, di' hon ta panta kai di' hou ta panta, pollous huious
   eis doxan agagonta ton archegon tes soterias auton dia pathematon
   teleiosai.

   ho te gar hagiazon kai hoi hagiazomenoi ex henos pantes· di' hen aitian
   ouk epaischunetai adelphous autous kalein,

   legon· Apangelo to onoma sou tois adelphois mou, en meso ekklesias
   humneso se·

   kai palin· Ego esomai pepoithos ep' auto· kai palin· Idou ego kai ta
   paidia ha moi edoken ho theos.

   Epei oun ta paidia kekoinoneken ?haimatos kai sarkos?, kai autos
   paraplesios meteschen ton auton, hina dia tou thanatou katargese ton to
   kratos echonta tou thanatou, tout' esti ton diabolon,

   kai apallaxe toutous, hosoi phobo thanatou dia pantos tou zen enochoi
   esan douleias.

   ou gar depou angelon epilambanetai, alla spermatos Abraam
   epilambanetai.

   hothen opheilen kata panta tois adelphois homoiothenai, hina eleemon
   genetai kai pistos archiereus ta pros ton theon, eis to hilaskesthai
   tas hamartias tou laou·

   en ho gar peponthen autos peirastheis, dunatai tois peirazomenois
   boethesai.
     __________________________________________________________________

   Hothen, adelphoi hagioi, kleseos epouraniou metochoi, katanoesate ton
   apostolon kai archierea tes homologias hemon ?Iesoun,

   piston onta to poiesanti auton hos kai Mouses ?en to oiko autou.

   pleionos gar ?houtos doxes? para Mousen exiotai kath' hoson pleiona
   timen echei tou oikou ho kataskeuasas auton·

   pas gar oikos kataskeuazetai hupo tinos, ho ?de panta kataskeuasas
   theos.

   kai Mouses men pistos en holo to oiko autou hos therapon eis marturion
   ton lalethesomenon,

   Christos de hos huios epi ton oikon autou· ?hos oikos esmen hemeis,
   ?ean ten parresian kai to kauchema tes ?elpidos kataschomen.

   Dio, kathos legei to pneuma to hagion· Semeron ean tes phones autou
   akousete,

   me sklerunete tas kardias humon hos en to parapikrasmo, kata ten
   hemeran tou peirasmou en te eremo,

   hou ?epeirasan hoi pateres humon ?en dokimasia? kai eidon ta erga mou

   tesserakonta ete· dio prosochthisa te genea ?taute kai eipon· Aei
   planontai te kardia· autoi de ouk egnosan tas hodous mou·

   hos omosa en te orge mou· Ei eiseleusontai eis ten katapausin mou.

   blepete, adelphoi, mepote estai en tini humon kardia ponera apistias en
   to apostenai apo theou zontos,

   alla parakaleite heautous kath' hekasten hemeran, achris hou to Semeron
   kaleitai, hina me sklerunthe ?tis ex humon? apate tes hamartias·

   metochoi gar ?tou Christou gegonamen?, eanper ten archen tes
   hupostaseos mechri telous bebaian kataschomen.

   en to legesthai· Semeron ean tes phones autou akousete, Me sklerunete
   tas kardias humon hos en to parapikrasmo.

   tines gar akousantes parepikranan; all' ou pantes hoi exelthontes ex
   Aiguptou dia Mouseos;

   tisin de prosochthisen tesserakonta ete; ouchi tois hamartesasin, hon
   ta kola epesen en te eremo;

   tisin de omosen me eiseleusesthai eis ten katapausin autou ei me tois
   apeithesasin;

   kai blepomen hoti ouk edunethesan eiselthein di' apistian.
     __________________________________________________________________

   Phobethomen oun mepote kataleipomenes epangelias eiselthein eis ten
   katapausin autou doke tis ex humon husterekenai·

   kai gar esmen euengelismenoi kathaper kakeinoi, all' ouk ophelesen ho
   logos tes akoes ekeinous, me ?sunkekerasmenous te pistei tois
   akousasin.

   eiserchometha gar ?eis katapausin hoi pisteusantes, kathos eireken· Hos
   omosa en te orge mou, Ei eiseleusontai eis ten katapausin mou, kaitoi
   ton ergon apo kataboles kosmou genethenton,

   eireken gar pou peri tes hebdomes houtos· Kai katepausen ho theos en te
   hemera te hebdome apo panton ton ergon autou,

   kai en touto palin· Ei eiseleusontai eis ten katapausin mou.

   epei oun apoleipetai tinas eiselthein eis auten, kai hoi proteron
   euangelisthentes ouk eiselthon di' apeitheian,

   palin tina horizei hemeran, Semeron, en Dauid legon meta tosouton
   chronon, kathos ?proeiretai, Semeron ean tes phones autou akousete, me
   sklerunete tas kardias humon·

   ei gar autous Iesous katepausen, ouk an peri alles elalei meta tauta
   hemeras.

   ara apoleipetai sabbatismos to lao tou theou·

   ho gar eiselthon eis ten katapausin autou kai autos katepausen apo ton
   ergon autou hosper apo ton idion ho theos.

   spoudasomen oun eiselthein eis ekeinen ten katapausin, hina me en to
   auto tis hupodeigmati pese tes apeitheias.

   Zon gar ho logos tou theou kai energes kai tomoteros huper pasan
   machairan distomon kai diiknoumenos achri merismou psuches ?kai
   pneumatos, harmon te kai muelon, kai kritikos enthumeseon kai ennoion
   kardias·

   kai ouk estin ktisis aphanes enopion autou, panta de gumna kai
   tetrachelismena tois ophthalmois autou, pros hon hemin ho logos.

   Echontes oun archierea megan dieleluthota tous ouranous, Iesoun ton
   huion tou theou, kratomen tes homologias·

   ou gar echomen archierea me dunamenon sumpathesai tais astheneiais
   hemon, ?pepeirasmenon de kata panta kath' homoioteta choris hamartias.

   proserchometha oun meta parresias to throno tes charitos, hina labomen
   eleos kai charin heuromen eis eukairon boetheian.
     __________________________________________________________________

   Pas gar archiereus ex anthropon lambanomenos huper anthropon
   kathistatai ta pros ton theon, hina prosphere dora te kai thusias huper
   hamartion,

   metriopathein dunamenos tois agnoousi kai planomenois epei kai autos
   perikeitai astheneian,

   kai ?di' auten? opheilei, kathos peri tou laou, houtos kai peri ?hautou
   prospherein ?peri hamartion.

   kai ouch heauto tis lambanei ten timen, alla kaloumenos hupo tou theou,
   ?kathosper kai Aaron.

   Houtos kai ho Christos ouch heauton edoxasen genethenai archierea, all'
   ho lalesas pros auton· Huios mou ei su, ego semeron gegenneka se·

   kathos kai en hetero legei· Su hiereus eis ton aiona kata ten taxin
   Melchisedek,

   hos en tais hemerais tes sarkos autou deeseis te kai hiketerias pros
   ton dunamenon sozein auton ek thanatou meta krauges ischuras kai
   dakruon prosenenkas kai eisakoustheis apo tes eulabeias,

   kaiper on huios, emathen aph' hon epathen ten hupakoen,

   kai teleiotheis egeneto ?pasin tois hupakouousin auto? aitios soterias
   aioniou,

   prosagoreutheis hupo tou theou archiereus kata ten taxin Melchisedek.

   Peri hou polus hemin ho logos kai dusermeneutos legein, epei nothroi
   gegonate tais akoais·

   kai gar opheilontes einai didaskaloi dia ton chronon, palin chreian
   echete tou didaskein humas ?tina ta stoicheia tes arches ton logion tou
   theou, kai gegonate chreian echontes galaktos, ?ou stereas trophes.

   pas gar ho metechon galaktos apeiros logou dikaiosunes, nepios gar
   estin·

   teleion de estin he sterea trophe, ton dia ten hexin ta aistheteria
   gegumnasmena echonton pros diakrisin kalou te kai kakou.
     __________________________________________________________________

   Dio aphentes ton tes arches tou Christou logon epi ten teleioteta
   pherometha, me palin themelion kataballomenoi metanoias apo nekron
   ergon, kai pisteos epi theon,

   baptismon ?didachen epitheseos te cheiron, anastaseos ?te nekron kai
   krimatos aioniou.

   kai touto ?poiesomen eanper epitrepe ho theos.

   Adunaton gar tous hapax photisthentas geusamenous te tes doreas tes
   epouraniou kai metochous genethentas pneumatos hagiou

   kai kalon geusamenous theou rhema dunameis te mellontos aionos,

   kai parapesontas, palin anakainizein eis metanoian, anastaurountas
   heautois ton huion tou theou kai paradeigmatizontas.

   ge gar he piousa ton ep' autes ?erchomenon pollakis? hueton, kai
   tiktousa botanen eutheton ekeinois di' ohus kai georgeitai,
   metalambanei eulogias apo tou theou·

   ekpherousa de akanthas kai tribolous adokimos kai kataras engus, hes to
   telos eis kausin.

   Pepeismetha de peri humon, agapetoi, ta kreissona kai echomena
   soterias, ei kai houtos laloumen·

   ou gar adikos ho theos epilathesthai tou ergou humon ?kai tes agapes
   hes enedeixasthe eis to onoma autou, diakonesantes tois hagiois kai
   diakonountes.

   epithumoumen de hekaston humon ten auten endeiknusthai spouden pros ten
   plerophorian tes elpidos achri telous,

   hina me nothroi genesthe, mimetai de ton dia pisteos kai makrothumias
   kleronomounton tas epangelias.

   To gar Abraam epangeilamenos ho theos, epei kat' oudenos eichen
   meizonos omosai, omosen kath' heautou,

   legon· ?Ei men eulogon eulogeso se kai plethunon plethuno se·

   kai houtos makrothumesas epetuchen tes epangelias.

   ?anthropoi gar kata tou meizonos omnuousin, kai pases autois antilogias
   peras eis bebaiosin ho horkos·

   en ho perissoteron boulomenos ho theos epideixai tois kleronomois tes
   epangelias to ametatheton tes boules autou emesiteusen horko,

   hina dia duo pragmaton ametatheton, en hois adunaton pseusasthai
   ?theon, ischuran paraklesin echomen hoi kataphugontes kratesai tes
   prokeimenes elpidos·

   hen hos ankuran echomen tes psuches, ?asphale te kai bebaian kai
   eiserchomenen eis to esoteron tou katapetasmatos,

   hopou prodromos huper hemon eiselthen Iesous, kata ten taxin
   Melchisedek archiereus genomenos eis ton aiona.
     __________________________________________________________________

   Houtos gar ho Melchisedek, basileus Salem, hiereus tou theou tou
   hupsistou, ?ho sunantesas Abraam hupostrephonti apo tes kopes ton
   basileon kai eulogesas auton,

   ho kai dekaten apo panton emerisen Abraam, proton men hermeneuomenos
   basileus dikaiosunes epeita de kai basileus Salem, ho estin basileus
   eirenes,

   apator, ametor, agenealogetos, mete archen hemeron mete zoes telos
   echon, aphomoiomenos de to huio tou theou, menei hiereus eis to
   dienekes.

   Theoreite de pelikos houtos ?ho dekaten Abraam edoken ek ton
   akrothinion ho patriarches.

   kai hoi men ek ton huion Leui ten hierateian lambanontes entolen
   echousin apodekatoun ton laon kata ton nomon, tout' estin tous
   adelphous auton, kaiper exeleluthotas ek tes osphuos Abraam·

   ho de me genealogoumenos ex auton dedekatoken ?Abraam, kai ton echonta
   tas epangelias eulogeken.

   choris de pases antilogias to elatton hupo tou kreittonos eulogeitai.

   kai hode men dekatas apothneskontes anthropoi lambanousin, ekei de
   marturoumenos hoti ze.

   kai hos epos eipein, di' Abraam kai Leui ho dekatas lambanon
   dedekatotai,

   eti gar en te osphui tou patros en hote sunentesen auto ?Melchisedek.

   Ei men oun teleiosis dia tes Leuitikes hierosunes en, ho laos gar ep'
   ?autes ?nenomothetetai, tis eti chreia kata ten taxin Melchisedek
   heteron anistasthai hierea kai ou kata ten taxin Aaron legesthai;

   metatithemenes gar tes hierosunes ex anankes kai nomou metathesis
   ginetai.

   eph' hon gar legetai tauta phules heteras metescheken, aph' hes oudeis
   prosescheken to thusiasterio·

   prodelon gar hoti ex Iouda anatetalken ho kurios hemon, eis hen phulen
   ?peri hiereon ouden? Mouses elalesen.

   Kai perissoteron eti katadelon estin, ei kata ten homoioteta
   Melchisedek anistatai hiereus heteros,

   hos ou kata nomon entoles ?sarkines gegonen alla kata dunamin zoes
   akatalutou,

   ?martureitai gar hoti Su hiereus eis ton aiona kata ten taxin
   Melchisedek.

   athetesis men gar ginetai proagouses entoles dia to autes asthenes kai
   anopheles,

   ouden gar eteleiosen ho nomos, epeisagoge de kreittonos elpidos, di'
   hes engizomen to theo.

   Kai kath' hoson ou choris horkomosias (hoi men gar choris horkomosias
   eisin hiereis gegonotes,

   ho de meta horkomosias dia tou legontos pros auton· Omosen kurios, kai
   ou metamelethesetai, Su hiereus eis ton ?aiona),

   kata ?tosouto ?kreittonos diathekes gegonen enguos Iesous.

   Kai hoi men pleiones eisin gegonotes hiereis dia to thanato koluesthai
   paramenein·

   ho de dia to menein auton eis ton aiona aparabaton echei ten
   hierosunen·

   hothen kai sozein eis to panteles dunatai tous proserchomenous di'
   autou to theo, pantote zon eis to entunchanein huper auton.

   Toioutos gar hemin ?kai eprepen archiereus, hosios, akakos, amiantos,
   kechorismenos apo ton hamartolon, kai hupseloteros ton ouranon
   genomenos·

   hos ouk echei kath' hemeran ananken, hosper hoi archiereis, proteron
   huper ton idion hamartion thusias anapherein, epeita ton tou laou
   (touto gar epoiesen ephapax heauton anenenkas)·

   ho nomos gar anthropous kathistesin archiereis echontas astheneian, ho
   logos de tes horkomosias tes meta ton nomon huion, eis ton aiona
   teteleiomenon.
     __________________________________________________________________

   Kephalaion de epi tois legomenois, toiouton echomen archierea, hos
   ekathisen en dexia tou thronou tes megalosunes en tois ouranois,

   ton hagion leitourgos kai tes skenes tes alethines, hen epexen ho
   kurios, ?ouk anthropos.

   pas gar archiereus eis to prospherein dora te kai thusias kathistatai·
   hothen anankaion echein ti kai touton ho prosenenke.

   ei men ?oun en epi ges, oud' an en hiereus, ?onton ton prospheronton
   kata ?nomon ta dora·

   (hoitines hupodeigmati kai skia latreuousin ton epouranion, kathos
   kechrematistai Mouses mellon epitelein ten skenen, Hora gar, phesin,
   poieseis panta kata ton tupon ton deichthenta soi en to orei)·

   ?nuni de diaphoroteras tetuchen leitourgias, hoso kai kreittonos estin
   diathekes mesites, hetis epi kreittosin epangeliais nenomothetetai.

   Ei gar he prote ekeine en amemptos, ouk an deuteras ezeteito topos·

   memphomenos gar ?autous legei· Idou hemerai erchontai, legei kurios,
   kai sunteleso epi ton oikon Israel kai epi ton oikon Iouda diatheken
   kainen,

   ou kata ten diatheken hen epoiesa tois patrasin auton en hemera
   epilabomenou mou tes cheiros auton exagagein autous ek ges Aiguptou,
   hoti autoi ouk enemeinan en te diatheke mou, kago emelesa auton, legei
   kurios.

   hoti haute he diatheke hen diathesomai to oiko Israel meta tas hemeras
   ekeinas, legei kurios, didous nomous mou eis ten dianoian auton, kai
   epi kardias auton epigrapso autous, kai esomai autois eis theon kai
   autoi esontai moi eis laon.

   kai ou me didaxosin hekastos ton politen autou kai hekastos ton
   adelphon autou, legon· Gnothi ton kurion, hoti pantes eidesousin me apo
   ?mikrou heos megalou auton.

   hoti hileos esomai tais adikiais auton, kai ton hamartion ?auton ou me
   mnestho eti.

   en to legein Kainen pepalaioken ten proten, to de palaioumenon kai
   geraskon engus aphanismou.
     __________________________________________________________________

   Eiche men ?oun he prote dikaiomata latreias to te hagion kosmikon.

   skene gar kateskeuasthe he prote en he he te luchnia kai he trapeza kai
   he prothesis ton arton, hetis legetai Hagia·

   meta de to deuteron katapetasma skene he legomene ?Hagia Hagion?,

   chrusoun echousa thumiaterion kai ten kiboton tes diathekes
   perikekalummenen pantothen chrusio, en he stamnos chruse echousa to
   manna kai he rhabdos Aaron he blastesasa kai hai plakes tes diathekes,

   huperano de autes Cheroubin doxes kataskiazonta to hilasterion· peri
   hon ouk estin nun legein kata meros.

   Touton de houtos kateskeuasmenon, eis men ten proten skenen dia pantos
   eisiasin hoi hiereis tas latreias epitelountes,

   eis de ten deuteran hapax tou eniautou monos ho archiereus, ou choris
   haimatos, ho prospherei huper heautou kai ton tou laou agnoematon,

   touto delountos tou pneumatos tou hagiou, mepo pephanerosthai ten ton
   hagion hodon eti tes protes skenes echouses stasin,

   hetis parabole eis ton kairon ton enestekota, kath' ?hen dora te kai
   thusiai prospherontai me dunamenai kata suneidesin teleiosai ton
   latreuonta,

   monon epi bromasin kai pomasin kai diaphorois baptismois, ?dikaiomata
   sarkos mechri kairou diorthoseos epikeimena.

   Christos de paragenomenos archiereus ton ?genomenon agathon dia tes
   meizonos kai teleioteras skenes ou cheiropoietou, tout' estin ou tautes
   tes ktiseos,

   oude di' haimatos tragon kai moschon dia de tou idiou haimatos,
   eiselthen ephapax eis ta hagia, aionian lutrosin heuramenos.

   ei gar to haima ?tragon kai tauron? kai spodos damaleos rhantizousa
   tous kekoinomenous hagiazei pros ten tes sarkos katharoteta,

   poso mallon to haima tou Christou, hos dia pneumatos aioniou heauton
   prosenenken amomon to theo, kathariei ten suneidesin ?hemon apo nekron
   ergon eis to latreuein theo zonti.

   Kai dia touto diathekes kaines mesites estin, hopos thanatou genomenou
   eis apolutrosin ton epi te prote diatheke parabaseon ten epangelian
   labosin hoi keklemenoi tes aioniou kleronomias.

   hopou gar diatheke, thanaton ananke pheresthai tou diathemenou·

   diatheke gar epi nekrois bebaia, epei ?mepote ischuei hote ze ho
   diathemenos.

   hothen oude he prote choris haimatos enkekainistai·

   laletheises gar pases entoles kata ?ton nomon hupo Mouseos panti to
   lao, labon to haima ton ?moschon meta hudatos kai eriou kokkinou kai
   hussopou auto te to biblion kai panta ton laon erantisen,

   legon· Touto to haima tes diathekes hes eneteilato pros humas ho theos·

   kai ten skenen de kai panta ta skeue tes leitourgias to haimati homoios
   erantisen.

   kai schedon en haimati panta katharizetai kata ton nomon, kai choris
   haimatekchusias ou ginetai aphesis.

   Ananke oun ta men hupodeigmata ton en tois ouranois toutois
   katharizesthai, auta de ta epourania kreittosi thusiais para tautas.

   ou gar eis cheiropoieta ?eiselthen hagia? Christos, antitupa ton
   alethinon, all' eis auton ton ouranon, nun emphanisthenai to prosopo
   tou theou huper hemon·

   oud' hina pollakis prosphere heauton, hosper ho archiereus eiserchetai
   eis ta hagia kat' eniauton en haimati allotrio,

   epei edei auton pollakis pathein apo kataboles kosmou· ?nuni de hapax
   epi sunteleia ton aionon eis athetesin ?hamartias dia tes thusias autou
   pephanerotai.

   kai kath' hoson apokeitai tois anthropois hapax apothanein, meta de
   touto krisis,

   houtos kai ho Christos, hapax prosenechtheis eis to pollon anenenkein
   hamartias, ek deuterou choris hamartias ophthesetai tois auton
   apekdechomenois eis soterian.
     __________________________________________________________________

   Skian gar echon ho nomos ton mellonton agathon, ouk auten ten eikona
   ton pragmaton, kat' eniauton tais autais thusiais has prospherousin eis
   to dienekes oudepote ?dunatai tous proserchomenous teleiosai·

   epei ouk an epausanto prospheromenai, dia to medemian echein eti
   suneidesin hamartion tous latreuontas hapax ?kekatharismenous;

   all' en autais anamnesis hamartion kat' eniauton,

   adunaton gar haima tauron kai tragon aphairein hamartias.

   dio eiserchomenos eis ton kosmon legei· Thusian kai prosphoran ouk
   ethelesas, soma de katertiso moi·

   holokautomata kai peri hamartias ouk eudokesas.

   tote eipon· Idou heko, en kephalidi bibliou gegraptai peri emou, tou
   poiesai, ho theos, to thelema sou.

   anoteron legon hoti ?Thusias kai prosphoras? kai holokautomata kai peri
   hamartias ouk ethelesas oude eudokesas, haitines kata ?nomon
   prospherontai,

   tote eireken· Idou heko tou ?poiesai to thelema sou· anairei to proton
   hina to deuteron stese.

   en ho thelemati hegiasmenoi ?esmen dia tes prosphoras tou somatos Iesou
   Christou ephapax.

   Kai pas men hiereus hesteken kath' hemeran leitourgon kai tas autas
   pollakis prospheron thusias, haitines oudepote dunantai perielein
   hamartias.

   ?houtos de mian huper hamartion prosenenkas thusian eis to dienekes
   ekathisen en dexia tou theou,

   to loipon ekdechomenos heos tethosin hoi echthroi autou hupopodion ton
   podon autou,

   mia gar prosphora teteleioken eis to dienekes tous hagiazomenous.

   marturei de hemin kai to pneuma to hagion, meta gar to ?eirekenai·

   Haute he diatheke hen diathesomai pros autous meta tas hemeras ekeinas,
   legei kurios, didous nomous mou epi kardias auton, kai epi ?ten
   dianoian? auton epigrapso autous,

   ?kai ton hamartion auton kai ton anomion auton ou me ?mnesthesomai eti·

   hopou de aphesis touton, ouketi prosphora peri hamartias.

   Echontes oun, adelphoi, parresian eis ten eisodon ton hagion en to
   haimati Iesou,

   hen enekainisen hemin hodon prosphaton kai zosan dia tou
   katapetasmatos, tout' estin tes sarkos autou,

   kai hierea megan epi ton oikon tou theou,

   proserchometha meta alethines kardias en plerophoria pisteos,
   rherantismenoi tas kardias apo suneideseos poneras kai lelousmenoi to
   soma hudati katharo·

   katechomen ten homologian tes elpidos akline, pistos gar ho
   epangeilamenos·

   kai katanoomen allelous eis paroxusmon agapes kai kalon ergon,

   me enkataleipontes ten episunagogen heauton, kathos ethos tisin, alla
   parakalountes, kai tosouto mallon hoso blepete engizousan ten hemeran.

   Hekousios gar hamartanonton hemon meta to labein ten epignosin tes
   aletheias, ouketi peri hamartion apoleipetai thusia,

   phobera de tis ekdoche kriseos kai puros zelos esthiein mellontos tous
   hupenantious.

   athetesas tis nomon Mouseos choris oiktirmon epi dusin e trisin
   martusin apothneskei·

   poso dokeite cheironos axiothesetai timorias ho ton huion tou theou
   katapatesas, kai to haima tes diathekes koinon hegesamenos en ho
   hegiasthe, kai to pneuma tes charitos enubrisas.

   oidamen gar ton eiponta· Emoi ekdikesis, ego ?antapodoso· kai palin·
   ?Krinei kurios? ton laon autou.

   phoberon to empesein eis cheiras theou zontos.

   Anamimneskesthe de tas proteron hemeras, en hais photisthentes pollen
   athlesin hupemeinate pathematon,

   touto men oneidismois te kai thlipsesin theatrizomenoi, touto de
   koinonoi ton houtos anastrephomenon genethentes·

   kai gar tois ?desmiois sunepathesate, kai ten harpagen ton huparchonton
   humon meta charas prosedexasthe, ginoskontes echein ?heautous kreittona
   ?huparxin kai menousan.

   me apobalete oun ten parresian humon, hetis echei ?megalen
   misthapodosian?,

   hupomones gar echete chreian hina to thelema tou theou poiesantes
   komisesthe ten epangelian·

   eti gar mikron hoson hoson, ho erchomenos hexei kai ou chronisei·

   ho de dikaios ?mou ek pisteos zesetai, kai ean huposteiletai, ouk
   eudokei he psuche mou en auto.

   hemeis de ouk esmen hupostoles eis apoleian, alla pisteos eis
   peripoiesin psuches.
     __________________________________________________________________

   Estin de pistis elpizomenon hupostasis, pragmaton elenchos ou
   blepomenon·

   en taute gar emarturethesan hoi presbuteroi.

   pistei nooumen katertisthai tous aionas rhemati theou, eis to me ek
   phainomenon ?to blepomenon? gegonenai.

   Pistei pleiona thusian Habel para Kain prosenenken to theo, di' hes
   emarturethe einai dikaios, marturountos epi tois dorois autou ?tou
   theou?, kai di' autes apothanon eti ?lalei.

   Pistei Henoch metetethe tou me idein thanaton, kai ouch heurisketo
   dioti metetheken auton ho theos· pro gar tes ?metatheseos memarturetai
   euarestekenai to theo,

   choris de pisteos adunaton euarestesai, pisteusai gar dei ton
   proserchomenon to theo hoti estin kai tois ekzetousin auton
   misthapodotes ginetai.

   pistei chrematistheis Noe peri ton medepo blepomenon eulabetheis
   kateskeuasen kiboton eis soterian tou oikou autou, di' hes katekrinen
   ton kosmon, kai tes kata pistin dikaiosunes egeneto kleronomos.

   ?Pistei kaloumenos Abraam hupekousen exelthein eis ?topon hon emellen
   lambanein eis kleronomian, kai exelthen me epistamenos pou erchetai.

   pistei parokesen eis gen tes epangelias hos allotrian, en skenais
   katoikesas meta Isaak kai Iakob ton sunkleronomon tes epangelias tes
   autes·

   exedecheto gar ten tous themelious echousan polin, hes technites kai
   demiourgos ho theos.

   pistei kai ?aute Sarra? dunamin eis katabolen spermatos elaben kai para
   kairon ?helikias, epei piston hegesato ton epangeilamenon·

   dio kai aph' henos egennethesan, kai tauta nenekromenou, kathos ta
   astra tou ouranou to plethei kai hos he ammos he para to cheilos tes
   thalasses he anarithmetos.

   Kata pistin apethanon houtoi pantes, me ?labontes tas epangelias, alla
   porrothen autas idontes kai aspasamenoi, kai homologesantes hoti xenoi
   kai parepidemoi eisin epi tes ges.

   hoi gar toiauta legontes emphanizousin hoti patrida epizetousin.

   kai ei men ekeines ?mnemoneuousin aph' hes ?exebesan, eichon an kairon
   anakampsai·

   nun de kreittonos oregontai, tout' estin epouraniou. dio ouk
   epaischunetai autous ho theos theos epikaleisthai auton, hetoimasen gar
   autois polin.

   Pistei prosenenochen Abraam ton Isaak peirazomenos, kai ton monogene
   prosepheren ho tas epangelias anadexamenos,

   pros hon elalethe hoti En Isaak klethesetai soi sperma,

   logisamenos hoti kai ek nekron egeirein dunatos ho theos· hothen auton
   kai en parabole ekomisato.

   Pistei ?kai peri mellonton eulogesen Isaak ton Iakob kai ton Esau.

   pistei Iakob apothneskon hekaston ton huion Ioseph eulogesen, kai
   prosekunesen epi to akron tes rhabdou autou.

   pistei Ioseph teleuton peri tes exodou ton huion Israel emnemoneusen,
   kai peri ton osteon autou eneteilato.

   Pistei Mouses gennetheis ekrube trimenon hupo ton pateron autou, dioti
   eidon asteion to paidion kai ouk ephobethesan to diatagma tou basileos.

   pistei Mouses megas genomenos ernesato legesthai huios thugatros
   Pharao,

   mallon helomenos sunkakoucheisthai to lao tou theou e proskairon echein
   hamartias apolausin,

   meizona plouton hegesamenos ton Aiguptou thesauron ton oneidismon tou
   Christou, apeblepen gar eis ten misthapodosian.

   pistei katelipen Aigupton, me phobetheis ton thumon tou basileos, ton
   gar aoraton hos horon ekarteresen.

   pistei pepoieken to pascha kai ten proschusin tou haimatos, hina me ho
   olothreuon ta prototoka thige auton.

   Pistei diebesan ten Eruthran Thalassan hos dia xeras ?ges, hes peiran
   labontes hoi Aiguptioi katepothesan.

   pistei ta teiche Iericho ?epesan kuklothenta epi hepta hemeras.

   pistei Rhaab he porne ou sunapoleto tois apeithesasin, dexamene tous
   kataskopous met' eirenes.

   Kai ti eti lego; epileipsei ?me gar? diegoumenon ho chronos peri
   Gedeon, Barak, ?Sampson, Iephthae, Dauid te kai Samouel kai ton
   propheton,

   ohi dia pisteos kategonisanto basileias, eirgasanto dikaiosunen,
   epetuchon epangelion, ephraxan stomata leonton,

   esbesan dunamin puros, ephugon stomata ?machaires, ?edunamothesan apo
   astheneias, egenethesan ischuroi en polemo, parembolas eklinan
   allotrion·

   elabon gunaikes ex anastaseos tous nekrous auton· alloi de
   etumpanisthesan, ou prosdexamenoi ten apolutrosin, hina kreittonos
   anastaseos tuchosin·

   heteroi de empaigmon kai mastigon peiran elabon, eti de desmon kai
   phulakes·

   elithasthesan, ?epristhesan, en phono ?machaires apethanon, perielthon
   en melotais, en aigeiois dermasin, husteroumenoi, thlibomenoi,
   kakouchoumenoi,

   hon ouk en axios ho kosmos ?epi eremiais planomenoi kai oresi kai
   spelaiois kai tais opais tes ges·

   ?kai pantes marturethentes dia tes pisteos ouk ekomisanto ten
   epangelian,

   tou theou peri hemon kreitton ti problepsamenou, hina me choris hemon
   teleiothosin.
     __________________________________________________________________

   Toigaroun kai hemeis, tosouton echontes perikeimenon hemin nephos
   marturon, onkon apothemenoi panta kai ten euperistaton hamartian, di'
   hupomones trechomen ton prokeimenon hemin agona,

   aphorontes eis ton tes pisteos archegon kai teleioten Iesoun, hos anti
   tes prokeimenes auto charas hupemeinen stauron aischunes kataphronesas,
   en dexia te tou thronou tou theou kekathiken.

   Analogisasthe gar ton toiauten hupomemenekota hupo ton hamartolon eis
   ?heautous antilogian, hina me kamete tais psuchais humon ekluomenoi.

   oupo mechris haimatos antikatestete pros ten hamartian antagonizomenoi,

   kai eklelesthe tes parakleseos, hetis humin hos huiois dialegetai, Huie
   mou, me oligorei paideias kuriou, mede ekluou hup' autou elenchomenos·

   hon gar agapa kurios paideuei, mastigoi de panta huion hon
   paradechetai.

   eis paideian hupomenete· hos huiois humin prospheretai ho theos· tis
   ?gar huios hon ou paideuei pater;

   ei de choris este paideias hes metochoi gegonasi pantes, ara nothoi
   ?kai ouch huioi este?.

   eita tous men tes sarkos hemon pateras eichomen paideutas kai
   enetrepometha· ou ?polu mallon hupotagesometha to patri ton pneumaton
   kai zesomen;

   hoi men gar pros oligas hemeras kata to dokoun autois epaideuon, ho de
   epi to sumpheron eis to metalabein tes hagiotetos autou.

   pasa ?de paideia pros men to paron ou dokei charas einai alla lupes,
   husteron de karpon eirenikon tois di' autes gegumnasmenois apodidosin
   dikaiosunes.

   Dio tas pareimenas cheiras kai ta paralelumena gonata anorthosate,

   kai trochias orthas ?poieite tois posin humon, hina me to cholon
   ektrape, iathe de mallon.

   Eirenen diokete meta panton, kai ton hagiasmon, hou choris oudeis
   opsetai ton kurion,

   episkopountes me tis husteron apo tes charitos tou theou, me tis rhiza
   pikrias ano phuousa enochle kai ?di' autes? mianthosin ?polloi,

   me tis pornos e bebelos hos Esau, hos anti broseos mias apedeto ta
   prototokia ?heautou.

   iste gar hoti kai metepeita thelon kleronomesai ten eulogian
   apedokimasthe, metanoias gar topon ouch heuren, kaiper meta dakruon
   ekzetesas auten.

   Ou gar proseleluthate ?pselaphomeno kai kekaumeno puri kai gnopho kai
   ?zopho kai thuelle

   kai salpingos echo kai phone rhematon, hes hoi akousantes paretesanto
   ?me prostethenai autois logon·

   ouk epheron gar to diastellomenon· Kan therion thige tou orous,
   lithobolethesetai·

   kai, houto phoberon en to phantazomenon, Mouses eipen· Ekphobos eimi
   kai entromos.

   alla proseleluthate Sion orei kai polei theou zontos, Ierousalem
   epouranio, kai muriasin angelon, panegurei

   kai ekklesia prototokon ?apogegrammenon en ouranois?, kai krite theo
   panton, kai pneumasi dikaion teteleiomenon,

   kai diathekes neas mesite Iesou, kai haimati rhantismou kreitton
   lalounti para ton Habel.

   Blepete me paraitesesthe ton lalounta· ei gar ekeinoi ouk ?exephugon
   ?epi ges paraitesamenoi ton? chrematizonta, ?polu mallon hemeis hoi ton
   ap' ouranon apostrephomenoi·

   hou he phone ten gen esaleusen tote, nun de epengeltai legon· Eti hapax
   ego ?seiso ou monon ten gen alla kai ton ouranon.

   to de Eti hapax deloi ?ton saleuomenon? metathesin hos pepoiemenon,
   hina meine ta me saleuomena.

   dio basileian asaleuton paralambanontes echomen charin, di' hes
   ?latreuomen euarestos to theo meta ?eulabeias kai deous?,

   kai gar ho theos hemon pur katanaliskon.
     __________________________________________________________________

   He philadelphia meneto.

   tes philoxenias me epilanthanesthe, dia tautes gar elathon tines
   xenisantes angelous.

   mimneskesthe ton desmion hos sundedemenoi, ton kakouchoumenon hos kai
   autoi ontes en somati.

   timios ho gamos en pasin kai he koite amiantos, pornous ?gar kai
   moichous krinei ho theos.

   aphilarguros ho tropos· arkoumenoi tois parousin· autos gar eireken· Ou
   me se ano oud' ou me se ?enkatalipo·

   hoste tharrountas hemas legein· Kurios emoi boethos, ?ou phobethesomai·
   ti poiesei moi anthropos;

   Mnemoneuete ton hegoumenon humon, hoitines elalesan humin ton logon tou
   theou, hon anatheorountes ten ekbasin tes anastrophes mimeisthe ten
   pistin.

   Iesous Christos echthes kai semeron ho autos, kai eis tous aionas.

   didachais poikilais kai xenais me parapheresthe· kalon gar chariti
   bebaiousthai ten kardian, ou bromasin, en hois ouk ophelethesan hoi
   ?peripatountes.

   echomen thusiasterion ex hou phagein ouk echousin exousian hoi te skene
   latreuontes.

   hon gar eispheretai zoon to haima peri hamartias eis ta hagia dia tou
   archiereos, touton ta somata katakaietai exo tes paremboles·

   dio kai Iesous, hina hagiase dia tou idiou haimatos ton laon, exo tes
   pules epathen.

   toinun exerchometha pros auton exo tes paremboles, ton oneidismon autou
   pherontes.

   ou gar echomen hode menousan polin, alla ten mellousan epizetoumen·

   di' autou ?oun anapheromen thusian aineseos dia pantos to theo, tout'
   estin karpon cheileon homologounton to onomati autou.

   tes de eupoiias kai koinonias me epilanthanesthe, toiautais gar
   thusiais euaresteitai ho theos.

   Peithesthe tois hegoumenois humon kai hupeikete, autoi gar agrupnousin
   huper ton psuchon humon hos logon apodosontes, hina meta charas touto
   poiosin kai me stenazontes, alusiteles gar humin touto.

   Proseuchesthe peri hemon, ?peithometha gar hoti kalen suneidesin
   echomen, en pasin kalos thelontes anastrephesthai.

   perissoteros de parakalo touto poiesai hina tachion apokatastatho
   humin.

   Ho de theos tes eirenes, ho anagagon ek nekron ton poimena ton probaton
   ton megan en haimati diathekes aioniou, ton kurion hemon Iesoun,

   katartisai humas en ?panti agatho eis to poiesai to thelema autou,
   poion en ?hemin to euareston enopion autou dia Iesou Christou, ho he
   doxa eis tous ?aionas· amen.

   Parakalo de humas, adelphoi, anechesthe tou logou tes parakleseos, kai
   gar dia bracheon epesteila humin.

   ginoskete ton adelphon ?hemon Timotheon apolelumenon, meth' hou ean
   tachion erchetai opsomai humas.

   aspasasthe pantas tous hegoumenous humon kai pantas tous hagious.
   aspazontai humas hoi apo tes Italias.

   he charis meta panton ?humon.
     __________________________________________________________________

                                    IAKOBOU
     __________________________________________________________________

   Iakobos theou kai kuriou Iesou Christou doulos tais dodeka phulais tais
   en te diaspora chairein.

   Pasan charan hegesasthe, adelphoi mou, hotan peirasmois peripesete
   poikilois,

   ginoskontes hoti to dokimion humon tes pisteos katergazetai hupomonen·

   he de hupomone ergon teleion echeto, hina ete teleioi kai holokleroi,
   en medeni leipomenoi.

   Ei de tis humon leipetai sophias, aiteito para tou didontos theou pasin
   haplos kai ?me oneidizontos, kai dothesetai auto·

   aiteito de en pistei, meden diakrinomenos, ho gar diakrinomenos eoiken
   kludoni thalasses anemizomeno kai rhipizomeno·

   me gar oiestho ho anthropos ekeinos hoti lempsetai ti para tou kuriou

   aner dipsuchos, akatastatos en pasais tais hodois autou.

   Kauchastho de ho adelphos ho tapeinos en to hupsei autou,

   ho de plousios en te tapeinosei autou, hoti hos anthos chortou
   pareleusetai.

   aneteilen gar ho helios sun to kausoni kai exeranen ton chorton, kai to
   anthos autou exepesen kai he euprepeia tou prosopou autou apoleto·
   houtos kai ho plousios en tais poreiais autou maranthesetai.

   Makarios aner hos hupomenei peirasmon, hoti dokimos genomenos lempsetai
   ton stephanon tes zoes, hon ?epengeilato tois agaposin auton.

   medeis peirazomenos legeto hoti Apo theou peirazomai· ho gar theos
   apeirastos estin kakon, peirazei de autos oudena.

   hekastos de peirazetai hupo tes idias epithumias exelkomenos kai
   deleazomenos·

   eita he epithumia sullabousa tiktei hamartian, he de hamartia
   apotelestheisa apokuei thanaton.

   me planasthe, adelphoi mou agapetoi.

   Pasa dosis agathe kai pan dorema teleion anothen estin, katabainon apo
   tou patros ton photon, par' ho ouk eni parallage e tropes aposkiasma.

   bouletheis apekuesen hemas logo aletheias, eis to einai hemas aparchen
   tina ton autou ktismaton.

   ?Iste, adelphoi mou agapetoi. esto ?de pas anthropos tachus eis to
   akousai, bradus eis to lalesai, bradus eis orgen,

   orge gar andros dikaiosunen theou ?ouk ergazetai?.

   dio apothemenoi pasan rhuparian kai perisseian kakias en prauteti
   dexasthe ton emphuton logon ton dunamenon sosai tas psuchas humon.

   Ginesthe de poietai logou kai me ?akroatai monon? paralogizomenoi
   heautous.

   hoti ei tis akroates logou estin kai ou poietes, houtos eoiken andri
   katanoounti to prosopon tes geneseos autou en esoptro,

   katenoesen gar heauton kai apeleluthen kai eutheos epelatheto hopoios
   en.

   ho de parakupsas eis nomon teleion ton tes eleutherias kai parameinas,
   ?ouk akroates epilesmones genomenos alla poietes ergou, houtos makarios
   en te poiesei autou estai.

   Ei tis dokei threskos ?einai me chalinagogon glossan ?autou alla apaton
   kardian ?autou, toutou mataios he threskeia.

   threskeia kathara kai amiantos para ?to theo kai patri haute estin,
   episkeptesthai orphanous kai cheras en te thlipsei auton, aspilon
   heauton terein apo tou kosmou.
     __________________________________________________________________

   Adelphoi mou, me en prosopolempsiais echete ten pistin tou kuriou hemon
   Iesou Christou tes doxes;

   ean gar eiselthe ?eis sunagogen humon aner chrusodaktulios en estheti
   lampra, eiselthe de kai ptochos en rhupara estheti,

   ?epiblepsete de? epi ton phorounta ten estheta ten lampran kai ?eipete·
   Su kathou hode kalos, kai to ptocho eipete· Su stethi ?e kathou ekei?
   hupo to hupopodion mou,

   ?ou diekrithete en heautois kai egenesthe kritai dialogismon poneron;

   akousate, adelphoi mou agapetoi. ouch ho theos exelexato tous ptochous
   ?to kosmo? plousious en pistei kai kleronomous tes basileias hes
   epengeilato tois agaposin auton;

   humeis de etimasate ton ptochon. ouch hoi plousioi katadunasteuousin
   humon, kai autoi helkousin humas eis kriteria;

   ouk autoi blasphemousin to kalon onoma to epiklethen eph' humas;

   Ei mentoi nomon teleite basilikon kata ten graphen Agapeseis ton
   plesion sou hos seauton, kalos poieite·

   ei de prosopolempteite, hamartian ergazesthe, elenchomenoi hupo tou
   nomou hos parabatai.

   hostis gar holon ton nomon ?terese, ptaise? de en heni, gegonen panton
   enochos.

   ho gar eipon Me ?moicheuses eipen kai Me ?phoneuses· ei de ou
   ?moicheueis phoneueis? de, gegonas parabates nomou.

   houtos laleite kai houtos poieite hos dia nomou eleutherias mellontes
   krinesthai.

   he gar krisis aneleos to me poiesanti eleos· katakauchatai ?eleos
   kriseos.

   ?Ti ophelos, adelphoi mou, ean pistin lege tis echein erga de me eche;
   me dunatai he pistis sosai auton;

   ?ean adelphos e adelphe gumnoi huparchosin kai ?leipomenoi tes
   ephemerou trophes,

   eipe de tis autois ex humon· Hupagete en eirene, thermainesthe kai
   chortazesthe, me dote de autois ta epitedeia tou somatos, ?ti ophelos;

   houtos kai he pistis, ean me ?eche erga?, nekra estin kath' heauten.

   All' erei tis· Su pistin echeis kago erga echo. deixon moi ten pistin
   sou ?choris ton ?ergon, kago ?soi deixo? ek ton ergon mou ten ?pistin.

   su pisteueis hoti ?heis estin ho theos?; kalos poieis· kai ta daimonia
   pisteuousin kai phrissousin.

   theleis de gnonai, o anthrope kene, hoti he pistis choris ton ergon
   ?arge estin;

   Abraam ho pater hemon ouk ex ergon edikaiothe, anenenkas Isaak ton
   huion autou epi to thusiasterion;

   blepeis hoti he pistis sunergei tois ergois autou kai ek ton ergon he
   pistis eteleiothe,

   kai eplerothe he graphe he legousa· Episteusen de Abraam to theo, kai
   elogisthe auto eis dikaiosunen, kai philos theou eklethe.

   ?horate hoti ex ergon dikaioutai anthropos kai ouk ek pisteos monon.

   homoios de kai Rhaab he porne ouk ex ergon edikaiothe, hupodexamene
   tous angelous kai hetera hodo ekbalousa;

   hosper ?gar to soma choris pneumatos nekron estin, houtos kai he pistis
   ?choris ergon nekra estin.
     __________________________________________________________________

   Me polloi didaskaloi ginesthe, adelphoi mou, eidotes hoti meizon krima
   lempsometha·

   polla gar ptaiomen hapantes. ei tis en logo ou ptaiei, houtos teleios
   aner, dunatos chalinagogesai kai holon to soma.

   ?ei de? ton hippon tous chalinous eis ta stomata ballomen ?eis to
   peithesthai autous hemin, kai holon to soma auton metagomen.

   idou kai ta ploia, telikauta onta kai hupo ?anemon skleron? elaunomena,
   metagetai hupo elachistou pedaliou hopou ?he horme tou euthunontos
   bouletai?·

   houtos kai he glossa mikron melos estin kai ?megala auchei?.

   Idou ?helikon pur heliken hulen anaptei·

   kai he glossa pur, ho kosmos tes ?adikias he glossa kathistatai en tois
   melesin hemon, he spilousa holon to soma kai phlogizousa ton trochon
   tes geneseos kai phlogizomene hupo tes geennes.

   pasa gar phusis therion te kai peteinon herpeton te kai enalion
   damazetai kai dedamastai te phusei te anthropine·

   ten de glossan oudeis ?damasai dunatai anthropon?· ?akatastaton kakon,
   meste iou thanatephorou.

   en aute eulogoumen ton ?kurion kai patera, kai en aute katarometha tous
   anthropous tous kath' homoiosin theou gegonotas·

   ek tou autou stomatos exerchetai eulogia kai katara. ou chre, adelphoi
   mou, tauta houtos ginesthai.

   meti he pege ek tes autes opes bruei to gluku kai to pikron;

   me dunatai, adelphoi mou, suke elaias poiesai e ampelos suka; ?oute
   halukon? gluku poiesai hudor.

   Tis sophos kai epistemon en humin; deixato ek tes kales anastrophes ta
   erga autou en prauteti sophias.

   ei de zelon pikron echete kai eritheian en te kardia humon, me
   katakauchasthe kai pseudesthe kata tes aletheias.

   ouk estin haute he sophia anothen katerchomene, alla epigeios,
   psuchike, daimoniodes·

   hopou gar zelos kai eritheia, ekei akatastasia kai pan phaulon pragma.

   he de anothen sophia proton men hagne estin, epeita eirenike, epieikes,
   eupeithes, meste eleous kai karpon agathon, ?adiakritos, anupokritos·

   karpos ?de dikaiosunes en eirene speiretai tois poiousin eirenen.
     __________________________________________________________________

   Pothen polemoi kai ?pothen machai en humin; ouk enteuthen, ek ton
   hedonon humon ton strateuomenon en tois melesin humon;

   epithumeite, kai ouk echete· phoneuete kai zeloute, kai ou dunasthe
   epituchein· machesthe kai polemeite. ouk echete dia to me aiteisthai
   humas·

   aiteite kai ou lambanete, dioti kakos aiteisthe, hina en tais hedonais
   humon dapanesete.

   ?moichalides, ouk oidate hoti he philia tou kosmou echthra tou theou
   estin; hos ?ean oun boulethe philos einai tou kosmou, echthros tou
   theou kathistatai.

   e dokeite hoti kenos he graphe legei· Pros phthonon epipothei to pneuma
   ho ?katokisen en hemin;

   meizona de didosin charin· dio legei· Ho theos huperephanois
   antitassetai tapeinois de didosin charin.

   hupotagete oun to theo· antistete de to diabolo, kai pheuxetai aph'
   humon·

   engisate to theo, kai ?engiei humin. katharisate cheiras, hamartoloi,
   kai hagnisate kardias, dipsuchoi.

   talaiporesate kai penthesate kai klausate· ho gelos humon eis penthos
   ?metatrapeto kai he chara eis katepheian·

   tapeinothete enopion ?kuriou, kai hupsosei humas.

   Me katalaleite allelon, adelphoi· ho katalalon adelphou ?e krinon ton
   adelphon autou katalalei nomou kai krinei nomon· ei de nomon krineis,
   ouk ei poietes nomou alla krites.

   heis ?estin nomothetes ?kai krites?, ho dunamenos sosai kai apolesai·
   su de tis ei, ?ho krinon? ton ?plesion;

   Age nun hoi legontes· Semeron ?e aurion ?poreusometha eis tende ten
   polin kai ?poiesomen ekei ?eniauton kai ?emporeusometha kai
   ?kerdesomen·

   hoitines ouk epistasthe ?to tes aurion ?poia he zoe humon· atmis gar
   ?este ?he pros oligon phainomene, ?epeita kai aphanizomene·

   anti tou legein humas· Ean ho kurios ?thelese, kai ?zesomen kai
   ?poiesomen touto e ekeino.

   nun de kauchasthe en tais alazoneiais humon· pasa kauchesis toiaute
   ponera estin.

   eidoti oun kalon poiein kai me poiounti, hamartia auto estin.
     __________________________________________________________________

   Age nun hoi plousioi, klausate ololuzontes epi tais talaiporiais humon
   tais eperchomenais.

   ho ploutos humon sesepen, kai ta himatia humon setobrota gegonen,

   ho chrusos humon kai ho arguros katiotai, kai ho ios auton eis
   marturion humin estai kai phagetai tas sarkas humon· hos pur
   ethesaurisate en eschatais hemerais.

   idou ho misthos ton ergaton ton amesanton tas choras humon ho
   ?aphusteremenos aph' humon krazei, kai hai boai ton therisanton eis ta
   ota Kuriou Sabaoth ?eiseleluthasin·

   etruphesate epi tes ges kai espatalesate, ethrepsate tas kardias ?humon
   en hemera sphages.

   katedikasate, ephoneusate ton dikaion. ouk antitassetai humin;

   Makrothumesate oun, adelphoi, heos tes parousias tou kuriou. idou ho
   georgos ekdechetai ton timion karpon tes ges, makrothumon ep' ?auto
   heos ?labe proimon kai opsimon.

   makrothumesate kai humeis, sterixate tas kardias humon, hoti he
   parousia tou kuriou engiken.

   me stenazete, ?adelphoi, kat' allelon?, hina me krithete· idou ho
   krites pro ton thuron hesteken.

   hupodeigma labete, ?adelphoi, tes kakopathias kai tes makrothumias tous
   prophetas, ohi elalesan ?en to onomati kuriou.

   idou makarizomen tous ?hupomeinantas· ten hupomonen Iob ekousate, kai
   to telos kuriou ?eidete, hoti polusplanchnos estin ?ho kurios? kai
   oiktirmon.

   Pro panton de, adelphoi mou, me omnuete, mete ton ouranon mete ten gen
   mete allon tina horkon· eto de humon to Nai nai kai to Ou ou, hina me
   ?hupo krisin? pesete.

   Kakopathei tis en humin; proseuchestho· euthumei tis; psalleto.

   asthenei tis en humin; proskalesastho tous presbuterous tes ekklesias,
   kai proseuxasthosan ep' auton aleipsantes ?auton elaio en to onomati
   tou kuriou·

   kai he euche tes pisteos sosei ton kamnonta, kai egerei auton ho
   kurios· kan hamartias e pepoiekos, aphethesetai auto.

   exomologeisthe ?oun allelois ?tas hamartias? kai ?euchesthe huper
   allelon, hopos iathete. polu ischuei deesis dikaiou energoumene.

   Elias anthropos en homoiopathes hemin, kai proseuche proseuxato tou me
   brexai, kai ouk ebrexen epi tes ges eniautous treis kai menas hex·

   kai palin proseuxato, kai ho ouranos ?hueton edoken? kai he ge
   eblastesen ton karpon autes.

   Adelphoi ?mou, ean tis en humin planethe apo tes aletheias kai
   epistrepse tis auton,

   ?ginosketo hoti ho epistrepsas hamartolon ek planes hodou autou sosei
   psuchen ?autou ek thanatou kai kalupsei plethos hamartion.
     __________________________________________________________________

                                    PETROU A
     __________________________________________________________________

   Petros apostolos Iesou Christou eklektois parepidemois diasporas
   Pontou, Galatias, Kappadokias, Asias, kai Bithunias,

   kata prognosin theou patros, en hagiasmo pneumatos, eis hupakoen kai
   rhantismon haimatos Iesou Christou· charis humin kai eirene
   plethuntheie.

   Eulogetos ho theos kai pater tou kuriou hemon Iesou Christou, ho kata
   to polu autou eleos anagennesas hemas eis elpida zosan di' anastaseos
   Iesou Christou ek nekron,

   eis kleronomian aphtharton kai amianton kai amaranton, teteremenen en
   ouranois eis humas

   tous en dunamei theou phrouroumenous dia pisteos eis soterian hetoimen
   apokaluphthenai en kairo eschato.

   en ho agalliasthe, oligon arti ei ?deon lupethentes en poikilois
   peirasmois,

   hina to dokimion humon tes pisteos ?polutimoteron chrusiou tou
   apollumenou dia puros de dokimazomenou heurethe eis epainon kai ?doxan
   kai timen? en apokalupsei Iesou Christou.

   hon ouk ?idontes agapate, eis hon arti me horontes pisteuontes de
   ?agalliasthe chara aneklaleto kai dedoxasmene,

   komizomenoi to telos tes pisteos ?humon soterian psuchon.

   Peri hes soterias exezetesan kai exeraunesan prophetai hoi peri tes eis
   humas charitos propheteusantes,

   eraunontes eis tina e poion kairon edelou to en autois pneuma Christou
   promarturomenon ta eis Christon pathemata kai tas meta tauta doxas·

   hois apekaluphthe hoti ouch heautois humin de diekonoun auta, ha nun
   anengele humin dia ton euangelisamenon ?humas pneumati hagio
   apostalenti ap' ouranou, eis ha epithumousin angeloi parakupsai.

   Dio anazosamenoi tas osphuas tes dianoias humon, nephontes teleios,
   elpisate epi ten pheromenen humin charin en apokalupsei Iesou Christou.

   hos tekna hupakoes, me suschematizomenoi tais proteron en te agnoia
   humon epithumiais,

   alla kata ton kalesanta humas hagion kai autoi hagioi en pase
   anastrophe genethete,

   dioti gegraptai ?hoti Hagioi ?esesthe, hoti ego ?hagios.

   Kai ei patera epikaleisthe ton aprosopolemptos krinonta kata to
   hekastou ergon, en phobo ton tes paroikias humon chronon anastraphete·

   eidotes hoti ou phthartois, argurio e chrusio, elutrothete ek tes
   mataias humon anastrophes patroparadotou,

   alla timio haimati hos amnou amomou kai aspilou Christou,

   proegnosmenou men pro kataboles kosmou, phanerothentos de ep' ?eschatou
   ton chronon di' humas

   tous di' autou ?pistous eis theon ton egeiranta auton ek nekron kai
   doxan auto donta, hoste ten pistin humon kai elpida einai eis theon.

   Tas psuchas humon hegnikotes en te hupakoe tes ?aletheias eis
   philadelphian anupokriton ?ek kardias allelous agapesate ektenos,

   anagegennemenoi ouk ek sporas phthartes alla aphthartou, dia logou
   zontos theou kai ?menontos·

   dioti pasa sarx hos chortos, kai pasa doxa ?autes hos anthos chortou·
   exeranthe ho chortos, kai to ?anthos exepesen·

   to de rhema kuriou menei eis ton aiona. touto de estin to rhema to
   euangelisthen eis humas.
     __________________________________________________________________

   Apothemenoi oun pasan kakian kai panta dolon kai ?hupokriseis kai
   phthonous kai pasas katalalias,

   hos artigenneta brephe to logikon adolon gala epipothesate, hina en
   auto auxethete ?eis soterian?,

   ?ei egeusasthe hoti chrestos ho kurios.

   Pros hon proserchomenoi, lithon zonta, hupo anthropon men
   apodedokimasmenon para de theo eklekton entimon

   kai autoi hos lithoi zontes oikodomeisthe oikos pneumatikos ?eis
   hierateuma hagion, anenenkai pneumatikas thusias ?euprosdektous theo
   dia Iesou Christou·

   dioti periechei ?en graphe· Idou tithemi en Sion lithon ?akrogoniaion
   eklekton? entimon, kai ho pisteuon ep' auto ou me kataischunthe.

   humin oun he time tois pisteuousin· ?apistousin de ?lithos hon
   apedokimasan hoi oikodomountes houtos egenethe eis kephalen gonias

   kai lithos proskommatos kai petra skandalou· ohi proskoptousin to logo
   apeithountes· eis ho kai etethesan.

   Humeis de genos eklekton, basileion hierateuma, ethnos hagion, laos eis
   peripoiesin, hopos tas aretas exangeilete tou ek skotous humas
   kalesantos eis to thaumaston autou phos·

   hoi pote ou laos nun de laos theou, hoi ouk eleemenoi nun de
   eleethentes.

   Agapetoi, parakalo hos paroikous kai parepidemous apechesthai ton
   sarkikon epithumion, haitines strateuontai kata tes psuches·

   ten anastrophen humon ?en tois ethnesin echontes kalen?, hina, en ho
   katalalousin humon hos kakopoion, ek ton kalon ergon ?epopteuontes
   doxasosi ton theon en hemera episkopes.

   ?Hupotagete pase anthropine ktisei dia ton kurion· eite basilei hos
   huperechonti,

   eite hegemosin hos di' autou pempomenois eis ekdikesin kakopoion
   epainon de agathopoion

   (hoti houtos estin to thelema tou theou, agathopoiountas phimoun ten
   ton aphronon anthropon agnosian)·

   hos eleutheroi, kai me hos epikalumma echontes tes kakias ten
   eleutherian, all' hos ?theou douloi?.

   pantas timesate, ten adelphoteta ?agapate, ton theon phobeisthe, ton
   basilea timate.

   Hoi oiketai hupotassomenoi en panti phobo tois despotais, ou monon tois
   agathois kai epieikesin alla kai tois skoliois.

   touto gar charis ei dia suneidesin theou hupopherei tis lupas paschon
   adikos·

   poion gar kleos ei hamartanontes kai kolaphizomenoi hupomeneite; all'
   ei agathopoiountes kai paschontes hupomeneite, touto charis para theo.

   eis touto gar eklethete, hoti kai Christos epathen huper ?humon, humin
   hupolimpanon hupogrammon hina epakolouthesete tois ichnesin autou·

   hos hamartian ouk epoiesen oude heurethe dolos en to stomati autou·

   hos loidoroumenos ouk anteloidorei, paschon ouk epeilei, paredidou de
   to krinonti dikaios·

   hos tas hamartias hemon autos anenenken en to somati autou epi to
   xulon, hina tais hamartiais apogenomenoi te dikaiosune zesomen· hou to
   ?molopi iathete.

   ete gar hos probata ?planomenoi, alla epestraphete nun epi ton poimena
   kai episkopon ton psuchon humon.
     __________________________________________________________________

   ?Homoios gunaikes hupotassomenai tois idiois andrasin, hina ?kai ei
   tines apeithousin to logo dia tes ton gunaikon anastrophes aneu logou
   kerdethesontai

   epopteusantes ten en phobo hagnen anastrophen humon.

   hon esto ouch ho exothen emplokes trichon kai peritheseos chrusion e
   enduseos himation kosmos,

   all' ho kruptos tes kardias anthropos en to aphtharto tou ?praeos kai
   hesuchiou? pneumatos, ho estin enopion tou theou poluteles.

   houtos gar pote kai hai hagiai gunaikes hai elpizousai ?eis theon
   ekosmoun heautas, hupotassomenai tois idiois andrasin,

   hos Sarra ?hupekousen to Abraam, kurion auton kalousa· hes egenethete
   tekna agathopoiousai kai me phoboumenai medemian ptoesin.

   Hoi andres homoios sunoikountes kata gnosin, hos asthenestero skeuei to
   gunaikeio aponemontes timen, hos kai ?sunkleronomois charitos zoes, eis
   to me enkoptesthai tas proseuchas humon.

   To de telos pantes homophrones, sumpatheis, philadelphoi, eusplanchnoi,
   ?tapeinophrones,

   me apodidontes kakon anti kakou e loidorian anti loidorias tounantion
   de ?eulogountes, hoti eis touto eklethete hina eulogian kleronomesete.

   ho gar thelon zoen agapan kai idein hemeras agathas pausato ten
   ?glossan apo kakou kai ?cheile tou me lalesai dolon,

   ekklinato ?de apo kakou kai poiesato agathon, zetesato eirenen kai
   dioxato auten·

   hoti ophthalmoi kuriou epi dikaious kai ota autou eis deesin auton,
   prosopon de kuriou epi poiountas kaka.

   Kai tis ho kakoson humas ean tou agathou ?zelotai genesthe;

   all' ei kai paschoite dia dikaiosunen, makarioi. ton de phobon auton me
   phobethete mede tarachthete,

   kurion de ton ?Christon hagiasate en tais kardiais humon, ?hetoimoi aei
   pros apologian panti to aitounti humas logon peri tes en humin elpidos,

   ?alla meta prautetos kai phobou, suneidesin echontes agathen, hina en
   ho ?katalaleisthe kataischunthosin hoi epereazontes humon ten agathen
   en Christo anastrophen.

   kreitton gar agathopoiountas, ei theloi to thelema tou theou, paschein
   e kakopoiountas.

   hoti kai Christos hapax peri hamartion ?epathen, dikaios huper adikon,
   hina ?humas prosagage to theo, thanatotheis men sarki zoopoietheis de
   pneumati·

   en ho kai tois en phulake pneumasin poreutheis ekeruxen,

   apeithesasin pote hote apexedecheto he tou theou makrothumia en
   hemerais Noe kataskeuazomenes kibotou eis hen ?oligoi, tout' estin okto
   psuchai, diesothesan di' hudatos.

   ho ?kai humas antitupon nun? sozei baptisma, ou sarkos apothesis rhupou
   alla suneideseos agathes eperotema eis theon, di' anastaseos Iesou
   Christou,

   hos estin en ?dexia theou poreutheis eis ouranon hupotagenton auto
   angelon kai exousion kai dunameon.
     __________________________________________________________________

   Christou oun ?pathontos sarki kai humeis ten auten ennoian hoplisasthe,
   hoti ho ?pathon sarki pepautai ?hamartias,

   eis to meketi anthropon epithumiais alla thelemati theou ton epiloipon
   en sarki biosai chronon.

   arketos ?gar ho pareleluthos ?chronos to ?boulema ton ethnon
   ?kateirgasthai, peporeumenous en aselgeiais, epithumiais,
   oinophlugiais, komois, potois, kai athemitois eidololatriais.

   en ho xenizontai me suntrechonton humon eis ten auten tes asotias
   anachusin, blasphemountes·

   ohi apodosousin logon to hetoimos ?echonti krinai? zontas kai nekrous·

   eis touto gar kai nekrois euengelisthe hina krithosi men kata
   anthropous sarki zosi de kata theon pneumati.

   Panton de to telos engiken. sophronesate oun kai nepsate ?eis
   proseuchas·

   pro ?panton ten eis heautous agapen ektene echontes, hoti agape
   ?kaluptei plethos hamartion·

   philoxenoi eis allelous aneu ?gongusmou·

   hekastos kathos elaben charisma, eis heautous auto diakonountes hos
   kaloi oikonomoi poikiles charitos theou·

   ei tis lalei, hos logia theou· ei tis diakonei, hos ex ischuos ?hes
   choregei ho theos· hina en pasin doxazetai ho theos dia Iesou Christou,
   ho estin he doxa kai to kratos eis tous aionas ton aionon· amen.

   Agapetoi, me xenizesthe te en humin purosei pros peirasmon humin
   ginomene hos xenou humin sumbainontos,

   alla katho koinoneite tois tou Christou pathemasin chairete, hina kai
   en te apokalupsei tes doxes autou charete agalliomenoi.

   ei oneidizesthe en onomati Christou, makarioi, hoti to tes doxes kai to
   tou theou pneuma eph' humas ?anapauetai.

   me gar tis humon pascheto hos phoneus e kleptes e kakopoios e hos
   allotriepiskopos·

   ei de hos Christianos, me aischunestho, doxazeto de ton theon en to
   ?onomati touto.

   hoti ho kairos tou arxasthai to krima apo tou oikou tou theou· ei de
   proton aph' hemon, ti to telos ton apeithounton to tou theou euangelio;

   kai ei ho dikaios molis sozetai, ?ho asebes kai hamartolos pou
   phaneitai;

   hoste kai hoi paschontes kata to thelema tou ?theou pisto ktiste
   paratithesthosan tas psuchas ?auton en agathopoiia.
     __________________________________________________________________

   Presbuterous ?oun en humin parakalo ho sumpresbuteros kai martus ton
   tou Christou pathematon, ho kai tes mellouses apokaluptesthai doxes
   koinonos,

   poimanate to en humin poimnion tou theou, ?episkopountes me anankastos
   alla hekousios ?kata theon?, mede aischrokerdos alla prothumos,

   med' hos katakurieuontes ton kleron alla tupoi ginomenoi tou poimniou·

   kai phanerothentos tou archipoimenos komieisthe ton amarantinon tes
   doxes stephanon.

   homoios, neoteroi, hupotagete presbuterois. pantes de ?allelois ten
   tapeinophrosunen enkombosasthe, hoti Ho theos huperephanois
   antitassetai tapeinois de didosin charin.

   Tapeinothete oun hupo ten krataian cheira tou theou, hina humas hupsose
   en kairo,

   pasan ten merimnan humon epiripsantes ep' auton, hoti auto melei peri
   humon.

   nepsate, gregoresate. ho antidikos humon diabolos hos leon oruomenos
   peripatei zeton ?tina ?katapiein·

   ho antistete stereoi te pistei, eidotes ta auta ton pathematon te en
   ?to kosmo humon adelphoteti epiteleisthai.

   ho de theos pases charitos, ho kalesas humas eis ten aionion autou
   doxan en ?Christo, oligon pathontas autos ?katartisei, sterixei,
   sthenosei, ?themeliosei.

   ?auto to kratos eis tous aionas ?ton aionon?· amen.

   Dia Silouanou humin tou pistou adelphou, hos logizomai, di' oligon
   egrapsa, parakalon kai epimarturon tauten einai alethe charin tou
   theou· eis hen ?stete.

   aspazetai humas he en Babuloni suneklekte kai Markos ho huios mou.

   aspasasthe allelous en philemati agapes. eirene humin pasin tois en
   ?Christo.
     __________________________________________________________________

                                    PETROU B
     __________________________________________________________________

   ?Sumeon Petros doulos kai apostolos Iesou Christou tois isotimon hemin
   lachousin pistin en dikaiosune tou theou hemon kai soteros Iesou
   Christou·

   charis humin kai eirene plethuntheie en epignosei tou theou kai Iesou
   tou kuriou hemon.

   Hos panta hemin tes theias dunameos autou ta pros zoen kai eusebeian
   dedoremenes dia tes epignoseos tou kalesantos hemas ?idia doxe kai
   arete?,

   di' hon ta ?timia kai megista hemin? epangelmata dedoretai, hina dia
   touton genesthe theias koinonoi phuseos, apophugontes tes en ?to kosmo
   en epithumia phthoras.

   kai auto touto de spouden pasan pareisenenkantes epichoregesate en te
   pistei humon ten areten, en de te arete ten gnosin,

   en de te gnosei ten enkrateian, en de te enkrateia ten hupomonen, en de
   te hupomone ten eusebeian,

   en de te eusebeia ten philadelphian, en de te philadelphia ten agapen·

   tauta gar humin huparchonta kai pleonazonta ouk argous oude akarpous
   kathistesin eis ten tou kuriou hemon Iesou Christou epignosin·

   ho gar me parestin tauta, tuphlos estin muopazon, lethen labon tou
   katharismou ton palai autou ?hamartematon.

   dio mallon, adelphoi, spoudasate bebaian humon ten klesin kai eklogen
   poieisthai· tauta gar poiountes ou me ptaisete pote·

   houtos gar plousios epichoregethesetai humin he eisodos eis ten aionion
   basileian tou kuriou hemon kai soteros Iesou Christou.

   Dio ?melleso aei humas hupomimneskein peri touton, kaiper eidotas kai
   esterigmenous en te parouse aletheia.

   dikaion de hegoumai, eph' hoson eimi en touto to skenomati, diegeirein
   humas en hupomnesei,

   eidos hoti tachine estin he apothesis tou skenomatos mou, kathos kai ho
   kurios hemon Iesous Christos edelosen moi·

   spoudaso de kai hekastote echein humas meta ten emen exodon ten touton
   mnemen poieisthai.

   Ou gar sesophismenois muthois exakolouthesantes egnorisamen humin ten
   tou kuriou hemon Iesou Christou dunamin kai parousian, all' epoptai
   genethentes tes ekeinou megaleiotetos.

   labon gar para theou patros timen kai doxan phones enechtheises auto
   toiasde hupo tes megaloprepous doxes· ?Ho huios mou ho agapetos mou
   houtos estin?, eis hon ego eudokesa--

   kai tauten ten phonen hemeis ekousamen ex ouranou enechtheisan sun auto
   ontes en to ?hagio orei?.

   kai echomen bebaioteron ton prophetikon logon, ho kalos poieite
   prosechontes hos luchno phainonti en auchmero topo, heos hou hemera
   diaugase kai phosphoros anateile en tais kardiais humon·

   touto proton ginoskontes hoti pasa propheteia graphes idias epiluseos
   ou ginetai,

   ou gar thelemati anthropou enechthe ?propheteia pote?, alla hupo
   pneumatos hagiou pheromenoi elalesan ?apo theou anthropoi.
     __________________________________________________________________

   Egenonto de kai pseudoprophetai en to lao, hos kai en humin esontai
   pseudodidaskaloi, hoitines pareisaxousin haireseis apoleias, kai ton
   agorasanta autous despoten arnoumenoi, epagontes heautois tachinen
   apoleian·

   kai polloi exakolouthesousin auton tais aselgeiais, di' ohus he hodos
   tes aletheias blasphemethesetai·

   kai en pleonexia plastois logois humas emporeusontai· hois to krima
   ekpalai ouk argei, kai he apoleia auton ou ?nustazei.

   Ei gar ho theos angelon hamartesanton ouk epheisato, alla ?seirais
   zophou tartarosas paredoken eis krisin teroumenous,

   kai archaiou kosmou ouk epheisato, alla ogdoon Noe dikaiosunes keruka
   ephulaxen, kataklusmon kosmo asebon epaxas,

   kai poleis Sodomon kai Gomorras tephrosas ?katastrophe katekrinen,
   hupodeigma mellonton ?asebesin tetheikos,

   kai dikaion Lot kataponoumenon hupo tes ton athesmon en aselgeia
   anastrophes errusato--

   blemmati gar kai akoe ?ho dikaios enkatoikon en autois hemeran ex
   hemeras psuchen dikaian anomois ergois ebasanizen--

   oiden kurios eusebeis ek peirasmou rhuesthai, adikous de eis hemeran
   kriseos kolazomenous terein,

   malista de tous opiso sarkos en epithumia miasmou poreuomenous kai
   kuriotetos kataphronountas.

   Tolmetai, authadeis, doxas ou tremousin, blasphemountes,

   hopou angeloi ischui kai dunamei meizones ontes ou pherousin kat'
   ?auton blasphemon krisin.

   houtoi de, hos aloga zoa ?gegennemena phusika? eis halosin kai
   phthoran, en hois agnoousin blasphemountes, en te phthora auton ?kai
   phtharesontai?,

   ?adikoumenoi misthon adikias· hedonen hegoumenoi ten en hemera truphen,
   spiloi kai momoi entruphontes en tais ?apatais auton suneuochoumenoi
   humin,

   ophthalmous echontes mestous moichalidos kai ?akatapaustous hamartias,
   deleazontes psuchas asteriktous, kardian gegumnasmenen pleonexias
   echontes, kataras tekna,

   ?katalipontes eutheian hodon eplanethesan, exakolouthesantes te hodo
   tou Balaam tou ?Bosor hos misthon adikias egapesen

   elenxin de eschen idias paranomias· hupozugion aphonon en anthropou
   phone phthenxamenon ekolusen ten tou prophetou paraphronian.

   Houtoi eisin pegai anudroi ?kai homichlai? hupo lailapos elaunomenai,
   hois ho zophos tou ?skotous teteretai.

   huperonka gar mataiotetos phthengomenoi deleazousin en epithumiais
   sarkos aselgeiais tous ?oligos ?apopheugontas tous en plane
   anastrephomenous,

   eleutherian autois epangellomenoi, autoi douloi huparchontes tes
   phthoras· ho gar tis hettetai, touto ?kai dedoulotai.

   ei gar apophugontes ta miasmata tou kosmou en epignosei tou ?kuriou kai
   soteros Iesou Christou toutois de palin emplakentes hettontai, gegonen
   autois ta eschata cheirona ton proton.

   kreitton gar en autois me epegnokenai ten hodon tes dikaiosunes e
   epignousin ?hupostrepsai ek tes paradotheises autois hagias entoles·

   ?sumbebeken autois to tes alethous paroimias· Kuon epistrepsas epi to
   idion exerama, kai· Hus lousamene eis ?kulismon borborou.
     __________________________________________________________________

   Tauten ede, agapetoi, deuteran humin grapho epistolen, en hais diegeiro
   humon en hupomnesei ten eilikrine dianoian,

   mnesthenai ton proeiremenon rhematon hupo ton hagion propheton kai tes
   ton apostolon humon entoles tou kuriou kai soteros,

   touto proton ginoskontes hoti eleusontai ep' ?eschaton ton hemeron ?en
   empaigmone? empaiktai kata tas idias epithumias auton poreuomenoi

   kai legontes· Pou estin he epangelia tes parousias autou; aph' hes gar
   hoi pateres ekoimethesan, panta houtos diamenei ap' arches ktiseos.

   lanthanei gar autous touto thelontas hoti ouranoi esan ekpalai kai ge
   ex hudatos kai di' hudatos sunestosa to tou theou logo,

   di' hon ho tote kosmos hudati kataklustheis apoleto·

   hoi de nun ouranoi kai he ge to ?auto logo tethesaurismenoi eisin puri
   teroumenoi eis hemeran kriseos kai apoleias ton asebon anthropon.

   Hen de touto me lanthaneto humas, agapetoi, hoti mia hemera para kurio
   hos chilia ete kai chilia ete hos hemera mia.

   ou bradunei ?kurios tes epangelias, hos tines braduteta hegountai, alla
   makrothumei eis ?humas, me boulomenos tinas apolesthai alla pantas eis
   metanoian choresai.

   hexei de ?hemera kuriou hos ?kleptes, en he hoi ouranoi rhoizedon
   pareleusontai, stoicheia de kausoumena ?luthesetai, kai ge kai ta en
   aute erga ?heurethesetai.

   Touton ?houtos panton luomenon potapous dei huparchein humas en hagiais
   anastrophais kai eusebeiais,

   prosdokontas kai speudontas ten parousian tes tou theou hemeras, di'
   hen ouranoi puroumenoi luthesontai kai stoicheia kausoumena teketai·

   kainous de ouranous kai gen kainen kata to epangelma autou prosdokomen,
   en hois dikaiosune katoikei.

   Dio, agapetoi, tauta prosdokontes spoudasate aspiloi kai amometoi auto
   heurethenai en eirene,

   kai ten tou kuriou hemon makrothumian soterian hegeisthe, kathos kai ho
   agapetos hemon adelphos Paulos kata ten ?dotheisan auto? sophian
   egrapsen humin,

   hos kai en pasais ?tais epistolais lalon en autais peri touton, en
   ?hais estin dusnoeta tina, ha hoi amatheis kai asteriktoi streblousin
   hos kai tas loipas graphas pros ten idian auton apoleian.

   humeis oun, agapetoi, proginoskontes phulassesthe hina me te ton
   athesmon plane sunapachthentes ekpesete tou idiou sterigmou,

   auxanete de en chariti kai gnosei tou kuriou hemon kai soteros Iesou
   Christou. auto he doxa kai nun kai eis hemeran aionos. ?amen.
     __________________________________________________________________

                                   IOANNOU A
     __________________________________________________________________

   Ho en ap' arches, ho akekoamen, ho heorakamen tois ophthalmois hemon,
   ho etheasametha kai hai cheires hemon epselaphesan, peri tou logou tes
   zoes--

   kai he zoe ephanerothe, kai heorakamen kai marturoumen kai apangellomen
   humin ten zoen ten aionion hetis en pros ton patera kai ephanerothe
   hemin--

   ho heorakamen kai akekoamen apangellomen ?kai humin, hina kai humeis
   koinonian echete meth' hemon· kai he koinonia de he hemetera meta tou
   patros kai meta tou huiou autou Iesou Christou·

   kai tauta graphomen ?hemeis hina he chara hemon e pepleromene.

   Kai estin haute he angelia hen akekoamen ap' autou kai anangellomen
   humin, hoti ho theos phos estin kai skotia ?en auto ouk estin? oudemia.

   ean eipomen hoti koinonian echomen met' autou kai en to skotei
   peripatomen, pseudometha kai ou poioumen ten aletheian·

   ean de en to photi peripatomen hos autos estin en to photi, koinonian
   echomen met' allelon kai to haima ?Iesou tou huiou autou katharizei
   hemas apo pases hamartias.

   ean eipomen hoti hamartian ouk echomen, heautous planomen kai he
   aletheia ?ouk estin en hemin?.

   ean homologomen tas hamartias hemon, pistos estin kai dikaios hina aphe
   hemin tas hamartias kai katharise hemas apo pases adikias.

   ean eipomen hoti ouch hemartekamen, pseusten poioumen auton kai ho
   logos autou ouk estin en hemin.
     __________________________________________________________________

   Teknia mou, tauta grapho humin hina me hamartete. kai ean tis hamarte,
   parakleton echomen pros ton patera Iesoun Christon dikaion,

   kai autos hilasmos estin peri ton hamartion hemon, ou peri ton
   hemeteron de monon alla kai peri holou tou kosmou.

   Kai en touto ginoskomen hoti egnokamen auton, ean tas entolas autou
   teromen.

   ho legon ?hoti Egnoka auton kai tas entolas autou me teron pseustes
   estin, kai en touto he aletheia ouk estin·

   hos d' an tere autou ton logon, alethos en touto he agape tou theou
   teteleiotai. en touto ginoskomen hoti en auto esmen·

   ho legon en auto menein opheilei kathos ekeinos periepatesen kai ?autos
   peripatein.

   ?Agapetoi, ouk entolen kainen grapho humin, all' entolen palaian hen
